Preliminaries
=============

We assume a fixed frame `F` on which to define the frame of nuclei.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="729" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="736" href="FrameOfNuclei.html" class="Module">FrameOfNuclei</a> <a id="750" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="751" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#751" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="753" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="755" href="Frame.html#3701" class="Function">Frame</a> <a id="761" href="Basis.html#2899" class="Generalizable">ğ’°</a> <a id="763" href="Basis.html#2901" class="Generalizable">ğ’±</a> <a id="765" href="Basis.html#2903" class="Generalizable">ğ’²</a><a id="766" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="768" class="Keyword">where</a>
</pre>
<pre class="Agda"><a id="787" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="792" href="Poset.html#3652" class="Module">PosetReasoning</a> <a id="807" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="808" href="Frame.html#3968" class="Function">pos</a> <a id="812" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#751" class="Bound">F</a><a id="813" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="815" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="821" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="822" href="Poset.html#3694" class="Function Operator">_âŠ‘âŸ¨_âŸ©_</a><a id="828" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="830" href="Poset.html#3832" class="Function Operator">_â– </a><a id="832" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
For simplicity, we will refer to the order, the meet, and the join of `F` simply
as `âŠ‘`, _âŠ“_`, and `â‹_`.

Poset of nuclei on `F` (`ğ”‘`)
============================

The set of endofunctions on a given frame forms a poset under the pointwise
order; we denote by `_âŠ‘f_` this pointwise order and by `ğ”‰` this poset.

We denote by `ğ”‘` the poset of nuclei:

    <a id="6544" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6544" class="Function">â¦…ğŸ’â¦†</a> <a id="6548" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6550" href="Frame.html#15010" class="Function">cleft</a>  <a id="6557" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#751" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="6559" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="6561" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6562" href="Frame.html#4933" class="Function Operator">âŠ“[</a> <a id="6565" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#751" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="6567" href="Frame.html#4933" class="Function Operator">]-lowerâ‚€</a> <a id="6576" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6577" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#5132" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="6579" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6580" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#5132" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="6582" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6043" class="Bound">x</a><a id="6583" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="6586" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6587" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#5132" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="6589" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6590" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#5162" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="6592" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6043" class="Bound">x</a><a id="6593" class="Symbol">)))</a>
    <a id="6601" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6601" class="Function">â¦…ğŸ“â¦†</a> <a id="6605" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6607" href="Frame.html#15010" class="Function">cleft</a>  <a id="6614" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#751" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="6616" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="6618" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6619" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#5150" class="Bound">j-nâ‚‚</a> <a id="6624" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6043" class="Bound">x</a><a id="6625" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="6631" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6631" class="Function">â¦…ğŸ”â¦†</a> <a id="6635" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6637" href="Frame.html#14652" class="Function">cright</a> <a id="6644" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#751" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="6646" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="6648" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6649" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#5180" class="Bound">k-nâ‚‚</a> <a id="6654" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6043" class="Bound">x</a><a id="6655" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
We now prove that `_âŠ“n_` is a greatest lower bound operator as expected:

<pre class="Agda"><a id="âŠ“n-meet"></a><a id="6744" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6744" class="Function">âŠ“n-meet</a> <a id="6752" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6754" href="Basis.html#1600" class="Function Operator">[</a> <a id="6756" href="Frame.html#1300" class="Function">isGLB</a> <a id="6762" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#2948" class="Function">ğ”‘</a> <a id="6764" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#5088" class="Function Operator">_âŠ“n_</a> <a id="6769" href="Basis.html#1600" class="Function Operator">]</a>

  <a id="6874" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6805" class="Function">lb</a> <a id="6877" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6878" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6878" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="6880" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="6882" class="Symbol">_)</a> <a id="6885" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6886" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6886" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="6888" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="6890" class="Symbol">_)</a> <a id="6893" class="Symbol">=</a>
    <a id="6899" class="Symbol">(Î»</a> <a id="6902" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6902" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="6904" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="6906" href="Frame.html#4933" class="Function Operator">âŠ“[</a> <a id="6909" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#751" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="6911" href="Frame.html#4933" class="Function Operator">]-lowerâ‚€</a> <a id="6920" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6921" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6878" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="6923" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6902" class="Bound">x</a><a id="6924" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6926" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6927" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6886" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="6929" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6902" class="Bound">x</a><a id="6930" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="6933" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="6935" class="Symbol">(Î»</a> <a id="6938" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6938" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="6940" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="6942" href="Frame.html#5063" class="Function Operator">âŠ“[</a> <a id="6945" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#751" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="6947" href="Frame.html#5063" class="Function Operator">]-lowerâ‚</a> <a id="6956" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6957" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6878" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="6959" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6938" class="Bound">x</a><a id="6960" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6962" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6963" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6886" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="6965" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6938" class="Bound">x</a><a id="6966" class="Symbol">))</a>

  <a id="6972" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6972" class="Function">greatest</a> <a id="6981" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6983" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6984" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6984" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="6986" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6986" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="6988" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6988" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="6990" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6992" href="Nucleus.html#578" class="Function">Nucleus</a> <a id="7000" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#751" class="Bound">F</a><a id="7001" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="7066" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#6972" class="Function">greatest</a> <a id="7075" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7076" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#7076" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="7078" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="7080" class="Symbol">_)</a> <a id="7083" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7084" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#7084" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="7086" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="7088" class="Symbol">_)</a> <a id="7091" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7092" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#7092" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="7094" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="7096" class="Symbol">_)</a> <a id="7099" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7100" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#7100" class="Bound">lâŠ‘j</a> <a id="7104" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="7106" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#7106" class="Bound">lâŠ‘k</a><a id="7109" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7111" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#7111" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="7113" class="Symbol">=</a>

</pre>
The meet of two Scott-continuous nuclei is itself Scott-continuous:

<pre class="Agda"><a id="âŠ“n-sc"></a><a id="7251" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#7251" class="Function">âŠ“n-sc</a> <a id="7257" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7259" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7260" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#7260" class="Bound">ğ’¿</a> <a id="7262" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#7262" class="Bound">ğ“€</a> <a id="7264" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7266" href="Nucleus.html#578" class="Function">Nucleus</a> <a id="7274" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#751" class="Bound">F</a><a id="7275" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7277" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="7279" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1345" class="Function">isScottCont</a> <a id="7291" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#7260" class="Bound">ğ’¿</a> <a id="7293" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="7295" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1345" class="Function">isScottCont</a> <a id="7307" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#7262" class="Bound">ğ“€</a> <a id="7309" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="7311" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1345" class="Function">isScottCont</a> <a id="7323" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7324" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#7260" class="Bound">ğ’¿</a> <a id="7326" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#5088" class="Function Operator">âŠ“n</a> <a id="7329" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#7262" class="Bound">ğ“€</a><a id="7330" class="Symbol">)</a>

</pre>
Using all these, we define the meet of two Scott-continuous nuclei.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="_âŠ“sc_"></a><a id="8563" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#8563" class="Function Operator">_âŠ“sc_</a> <a id="8569" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8571" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1795" class="Function">ScottContNucleus</a> <a id="8588" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="8590" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1795" class="Function">ScottContNucleus</a> <a id="8607" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="8609" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1795" class="Function">ScottContNucleus</a>

</pre>
which we verify to be a GLB operator as expected:

<pre class="Agda"><a id="âŠ“sc-meet"></a><a id="8765" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#8765" class="Function">âŠ“sc-meet</a> <a id="8774" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8776" href="Basis.html#1600" class="Function Operator">[</a> <a id="8778" href="Frame.html#1300" class="Function">isGLB</a> <a id="8784" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#3637" class="Function">ğ”–</a> <a id="8786" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#8563" class="Function Operator">_âŠ“sc_</a> <a id="8792" href="Basis.html#1600" class="Function Operator">]</a>

Arbitrary join of nuclei
------------------------

This is the non-trivial part of this development.

### Directification of a family of nuclei

We first define following function `â„œ` such that, given a family `U â‰” { fáµ¢ : A â†’
A âˆ£ i âˆˆ I }` of endofunctions, and a list `iâ‚€, â€¦, iâ‚™` of indices from `I`, `â„œ U
[iâ‚€, â€¦, iâ‚™]` denotes the composition `fáµ¢â‚™ âˆ˜ â‹¯ âˆ˜ fáµ¢â‚€`.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="â„œ"></a><a id="9283" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9283" class="Function">â„œ</a> <a id="9285" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9287" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9288" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9288" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="9290" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9292" href="Cubical.Core.Primitives.html#1230" class="Primitive">Type</a> <a id="9297" href="Basis.html#2450" class="Generalizable">â„“</a><a id="9298" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9300" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="9302" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9303" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9303" class="Bound">Î±</a> <a id="9305" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9307" href="Basis.html#5064" class="Function">Fam</a> <a id="9311" href="Basis.html#2452" class="Generalizable">â„“â€²</a> <a id="9314" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9315" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9288" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="9317" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="9319" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9288" class="Bound">A</a><a id="9320" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="9323" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="9325" href="Agda.Builtin.List.html#148" class="Datatype">List</a> <a id="9330" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9331" href="Basis.html#5139" class="Function">index</a> <a id="9337" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9303" class="Bound">Î±</a><a id="9338" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9340" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="9342" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9288" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="9344" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="9346" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9288" class="Bound">A</a>
<a id="9348" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9283" class="Function">â„œ</a> <a id="9350" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9350" class="Bound">Î±</a> <a id="9352" href="Agda.Builtin.List.html#185" class="InductiveConstructor">[]</a>       <a id="9361" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9363" href="Cubical.Foundations.Function.html#344" class="Function">idfun</a> <a id="9369" class="Symbol">_</a>
<a id="9371" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9283" class="Function">â„œ</a> <a id="9373" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9373" class="Bound">Î±</a> <a id="9375" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9376" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9376" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="9378" href="Agda.Builtin.List.html#200" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">âˆ·</a> <a id="9380" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9380" class="Bound">is</a><a id="9382" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9384" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9386" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9283" class="Function">â„œ</a> <a id="9388" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9373" class="Bound">Î±</a> <a id="9390" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9380" class="Bound">is</a> <a id="9393" href="Cubical.Foundations.Function.html#402" class="Function Operator">âˆ˜</a> <a id="9395" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9396" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9373" class="Bound">Î±</a> <a id="9398" href="Basis.html#5232" class="Function Operator">$</a> <a id="9400" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9376" class="Bound">i</a><a id="9401" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
Using `â„œ`, we define the family obtained from such a family of endofunctions
that consists of all such compositions.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="â„œ-fam"></a><a id="9534" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9534" class="Function">â„œ-fam</a> <a id="9540" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9542" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9543" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9543" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="9545" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9547" href="Cubical.Core.Primitives.html#1230" class="Primitive">Type</a> <a id="9552" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#761" class="Bound">ğ’°</a><a id="9553" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9555" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9556" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9556" class="Bound">Î±</a> <a id="9558" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9560" href="Basis.html#5064" class="Function">Fam</a> <a id="9564" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#765" class="Bound">ğ’²</a> <a id="9566" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9567" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9543" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="9569" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="9571" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9543" class="Bound">A</a><a id="9572" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="9575" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="9577" href="Basis.html#5064" class="Function">Fam</a> <a id="9581" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#765" class="Bound">ğ’²</a> <a id="9583" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9584" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9543" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="9586" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="9588" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9543" class="Bound">A</a><a id="9589" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="9591" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9534" class="Function">â„œ-fam</a> <a id="9597" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9598" class="Argument">A</a> <a id="9600" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9602" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9602" class="Bound">A</a><a id="9603" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9605" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9605" class="Bound">Î±</a> <a id="9607" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9609" href="Agda.Builtin.List.html#148" class="Datatype">List</a> <a id="9614" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9615" href="Basis.html#5139" class="Function">index</a> <a id="9621" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9605" class="Bound">Î±</a><a id="9622" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9624" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="9626" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9283" class="Function">â„œ</a> <a id="9628" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9605" class="Bound">Î±</a>
</pre>
We will use this function to compute the join of a family of nuclei. The key
idea is that the family of compositions is a directed family even if the family
we start with is not.

Notice that the identity function is always a (pre)nucleus.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="id-is-nuclear"></a><a id="9884" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9884" class="Function">id-is-nuclear</a> <a id="9898" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9900" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9901" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9901" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="9903" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9905" href="Frame.html#3701" class="Function">Frame</a> <a id="9911" href="Basis.html#2455" class="Generalizable">â„“â‚€</a> <a id="9914" href="Basis.html#2458" class="Generalizable">â„“â‚</a> <a id="9917" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#765" class="Bound">ğ’²</a><a id="9918" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9920" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="9922" href="Prenucleus.html#493" class="Function">isPrenuclear</a> <a id="9935" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9901" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="9937" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9938" href="Cubical.Foundations.Function.html#344" class="Function">idfun</a> <a id="9944" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">âˆ£</a> <a id="9946" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9901" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="9948" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">âˆ£F</a><a id="9950" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="9952" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9884" class="Function">id-is-nuclear</a> <a id="9966" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9966" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="9968" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9970" class="Symbol">(Î»</a> <a id="9973" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9973" class="Bound">_</a> <a id="9975" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9975" class="Bound">_</a> <a id="9977" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="9979" href="Cubical.Foundations.Prelude.html#898" class="Function">refl</a><a id="9983" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9985" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="9987" href="Poset.html#3014" class="Function Operator">âŠ‘[</a> <a id="9990" href="Frame.html#3968" class="Function">pos</a> <a id="9994" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#9966" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="9996" href="Poset.html#3014" class="Function Operator">]-refl</a>
</pre>
Compositions of prenuclei are prenuclei meaning given a family of nuclei, its
`â„œ-fam` is a family of prenuclei

<pre class="Agda"><a id="â„œ-fam-prenucleus"></a><a id="10128" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#10128" class="Function">â„œ-fam-prenucleus</a> <a id="10145" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10147" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10148" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#10148" class="Bound">K</a> <a id="10150" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10152" href="Basis.html#5064" class="Function">Fam</a> <a id="10156" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#765" class="Bound">ğ’²</a> <a id="10158" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10159" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">âˆ£</a> <a id="10161" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#751" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="10163" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">âˆ£F</a> <a id="10166" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="10168" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">âˆ£</a> <a id="10170" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#751" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="10172" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">âˆ£F</a><a id="10174" class="Symbol">))</a>

</pre>
For convenience, we introduce the following notation: given a some family
`J` of nuclei, `J ^*` denotes its `â„œ-fam`.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="_^*"></a><a id="11242" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#11242" class="Function Operator">_^*</a> <a id="11246" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11248" href="Basis.html#5064" class="Function">Fam</a> <a id="11252" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#765" class="Bound">ğ’²</a> <a id="11254" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11255" href="Nucleus.html#578" class="Function">Nucleus</a> <a id="11263" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#751" class="Bound">F</a><a id="11264" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="11266" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="11268" href="Basis.html#5064" class="Function">Fam</a> <a id="11272" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#765" class="Bound">ğ’²</a> <a id="11274" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11275" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">âˆ£</a> <a id="11277" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#751" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="11279" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">âˆ£F</a> <a id="11282" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="11284" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">âˆ£</a> <a id="11286" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#751" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="11288" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">âˆ£F</a><a id="11290" class="Symbol">)</a>

`J ^*` is always inhabited.

</pre>
Some nice notation for applying a certain nucleus in a family to an argument.

`J^*` is upwards-closed.

<a id="13594" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#13530" class="Function">J*-directed</a> <a id="13606" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#13606" class="Bound">J</a> <a id="13608" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="13610" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#12091" class="Function">J*-inhabited</a> <a id="13623" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#13606" class="Bound">J</a> <a id="13625" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="13627" class="Symbol">Î»</a> <a id="13629" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#13629" class="Bound">is</a> <a id="13632" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#13632" class="Bound">js</a> <a id="13635" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="13637" href="Basis.html#6953" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">âˆ£</a> <a id="13639" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#12762" class="Function">J*-up</a> <a id="13645" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#13606" class="Bound">J</a> <a id="13647" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#13629" class="Bound">is</a> <a id="13650" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#13632" class="Bound">js</a> <a id="13653" href="Basis.html#6953" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">âˆ£</a>
</pre>
Given a family `J` of Scott-continuous nuclei, everything in `J ^*` is
Scott-continuous.

Distributivity
--------------

We construct a rather involved proof of the fact that binary meets distribute
over arbitrary joins.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="dupl"></a><a id="21277" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#21277" class="Function">dupl</a> <a id="21282" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="21284" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="21285" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#21285" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="21287" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#21287" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="21289" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="21291" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">âˆ£</a> <a id="21293" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#751" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="21295" href="Frame.html#3884" class="Function Operator">âˆ£F</a><a id="21297" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="21299" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="21301" href="Basis.html#1600" class="Function Operator">[</a> <a id="21303" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#21285" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="21305" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1009" class="Function Operator">âŠ“</a> <a id="21307" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#21287" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="21309" href="Poset.html#2551" class="Function">âŠ‘[</a> <a id="21312" href="Frame.html#3968" class="Function">pos</a> <a id="21316" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#751" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="21318" href="Poset.html#2551" class="Function">]</a> <a id="21320" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#21285" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="21322" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1009" class="Function Operator">âŠ“</a> <a id="21324" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="21325" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#21285" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="21327" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#1009" class="Function Operator">âŠ“</a> <a id="21329" href="FrameOfNuclei.html#21287" class="Bound">y</a><a id="21330" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="21332" href="Basis.html#1600" class="Function Operator">]</a>
